# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="1ee72-105">.NET Framework 中過時的成員</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ee72-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1ee72-106">本文列出 .NET Framework 4.5 和更新版本中已過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ee72-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ee72-107">類型成員會依元件分組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ee72-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1ee72-108">本文不會列出過時的類型成員。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ee72-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1ee72-109">如需過時的類型清單，請參閱 [過時](obsolete-types.md)的型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ee72-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="1ee72-1111">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ee72-1111">IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
